[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The sanitizer report identifies a heap-buffer-overflow. A call to `strcmp` in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` reads three bytes from a buffer that was allocated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith only two bytes of addressable space.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m [0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Context  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The overflow occurs while parsing and identifying “maker note” data for Apple [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcameras. This path is reached via:  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in the fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_loader_fuzzer.cc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `exif_loader_get_data` in exif-loader.c  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `exif_data_load_data` and `interpret_maker_note` in exif-data.c  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` in apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The ASan trace shows the overflow during a `strcmp` call [0m[1;39m([0m[39m#[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe string terminator or comparison range exceeds the allocated region.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The two-byte region in question was allocated via `calloc` inside [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_alloc`, used to hold maker-note identification data.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The offending code path only appears in the Apple-specific maker-note handler [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`exif-mnote-data-apple.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting a mismatch between expected tag/data sizes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand what is actually allocated.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c: function `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` around[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m240[0m[39m  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • libexif/exif-data.c: functions `interpret_maker_note` and the data-loading [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • libexif/exif-loader.c: function `exif_loader_get_data` and any earlier size or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds computations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Calls to `exif_data_alloc` in exif-data.c to confirm allocation sizes versus [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bytes consumed by string comparisons  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis overflow points to a mismatch between the length of data expected by the Apple[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note identification logic and the length that is actually allocated, leading [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto reads beyond the heap buffer.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m151[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m152[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* v1 has offsets based to main IFD, not makernote IFD *[0m[35m/[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mdatao += n->offset + [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m154[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* subtract the size here, so the increment in the next case will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot harm us *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m*buf_size -= [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Fall through to nikonV2 handler *[0m[35m/[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:    [0m[39mcase nikonV2: [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Write out V0 files in V2 format *[0m[35m/[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[39m:    [0m[39mcase nikonV0: [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m*buf_size += [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m*buf_size += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Next IFD pointer *[0m[35m/[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m*buf = exif_mem_alloc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mne->mem, *buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!*buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mEXIF_LOG_NO_MEMORY[0m[1;39m([0m[39mne->log, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataOlympus"[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Write the header and the number of entries. *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mstrcpy [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*buf, [0m[32m"Nikon"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = n->version;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m: * format according to the EXIF specification, then it is converted to make it[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:static char *[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m74:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_olympus_get_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *d, unsigned int i, char *val, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned int maxlen[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:     [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi > n->count [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:     [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39md->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataOlympus"[0m[39m,[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"Querying value for tag '%s'..."[0m[39m,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[39m  mnote_olympus_tag_get_name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:     [0m[39mreturn mnote_olympus_entry_get_value [0m[1;39m([0m[39m&n->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, val, maxlen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m** [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m: * @brief save the MnoteData from ne to buf[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m: * [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m94[0m[39m: * @param ne extract the data from this structure [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m95[0m[39m: * @param *buf write the mnoteData to this buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer will be allocated[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m: * @param buf_size the size of the buffer[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m99:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_olympus_save [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *ne,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39munsigned char **buf, unsigned int *buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Apple maker-note identification function, [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_identify`, unconditionally calls `[0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39me->data, [0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `e->data` is allocated via `exif_data_alloc` with exactly `entry->size` bytes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mno extra byte for a NUL terminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `entry->size` is less than `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, `strcmp` overruns [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe heap buffer, triggering the heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Change the identification logic to a bounded comparison:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Do **not** rely on `strcmp`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - First verify that `e` and `e->data` are non-NULL and that `e->size` is at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleast as large as the signature length [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m bytes for `[0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use `memcmp` to compare exactly the [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m bytes of the signature, avoiding any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread past `entry->size`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserve existing functionality:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return the same `variant` values [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m for Apple, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m for non-Apple[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Do not alter any code outside `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Align with existing patterns:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Other maker-note handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., Olympus[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m perform a size check followed by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcmp`.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Follow that pattern to maintain consistency and avoid regressions.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the body of `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m236[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m246[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      #include <string.h>  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* for memcmp *[0m[35m/[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_apple_identify[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst ExifData *ed, const ExifEntry *e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          static const char apple_sig[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          const unsigned int sig_len = [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mapple_sig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Guard against NULL pointers and too-small buffers *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!e || !e->data || e->size < sig_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Compare only the first sig_len bytes *[0m[35m/[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmemcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[39me->data, apple_sig, sig_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          else[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure `<string.h>` is included at the top of the file if not already [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Bounded memory access: `memcmp` with an explicit length check eliminates any [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread outside the allocated buffer.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Minimal change: only one function is modified, so existing tests and harness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode remain untouched.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistency: other maker-note variants already use size checks and `memcmp`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso this approach matches the codebase style.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apple identification will only succeed if at least [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m bytes of data are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent. In the rare case where a valid Apple maker-note header is shorter than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely, since the spec uses `[0m[32m"Apple iOS"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it won’t be misdetected and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill fall through to other handlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno change from prior behavior for under-sized [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other part of the codebase is affected, as `exif_mnote_data_apple_identify`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis only invoked during maker-note recognition.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No Additional Files or Tests Modified[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzz harness, tests, and other source files remain unchanged.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix operates solely within the Apple maker-note identification routine and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserves the original dispatch logic in `interpret_maker_note`.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
